# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 08:57:56.683225

### Base Program

```py
def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def smooth_descent_periods(prices):
    count = 0
    i = 1
    while i < len(prices):
        if prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
            while i < len(prices) and prices[i] == prices[i - 1] - 1:
                i += 1
            count += 1
        else:
            i += 1
    return count


```
